**NOTES:**  
‚òõ Transponders data of Jeep Cherokee refers to all model versions: Cherokee Sport, Cherokee Limited, Cherokee Exclusive etc.  
‚òõ Transponders data of Jeep Grand Cherokee refers to all model versions: Grand Cherokee Laredo, Grand Cherokee Overland etc.  
‚òõ Some keys / transponders used in Jeep vehicles can be duplicated on "universal transponders" like XT27A66, K-JMD and others.  
Such "universal transponders" can emulate PCF7935, PCF7936, PCF7939, TEXAS 4C, TEXAS 4D and others.
